class="_ButtonInner_6dmow_4"><span class="">API Dashboard</span><svg width="1em" height="1em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="shrink-0"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.243 6.757a1 1 0 0 1 1 1v7.072a1 1 0 0 1-2 0v-4.657L8.464 16.95a1 1 0 0 1-1.414-1.414l6.778-6.779H9.172a1 1 0 0 1 0-2h7.07Z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></span></a></div> <div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-4 text-sm text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300 astro-3ef6ksr2">  </div> </div> </div> </div> </div>  <script>
  const MOBILE_NAV_PERSIST_KEY = "mobile-nav:restore-open";

  const readPersistedMobileNavOpen = () => {
    try {
      return sessionStorage.getItem(MOBILE_NAV_PERSIST_KEY) === "true";
    } catch {
      return false;
    }
  };

  const setPersistedMobileNavOpen = (isOpen) => {
    try {
      if (isOpen) {
        sessionStorage.setItem(MOBILE_NAV_PERSIST_KEY, "true");
      } else {
        sessionStorage.removeItem(MOBILE_NAV_PERSIST_KEY);
      }
    } catch {}
  };

  function initializeMobileNavigation() {
    const drawer = document.getElementById("drawer");
    const drawerButton = document.getElementById("header-drawer-button");

    if (
      !drawer ||
      !drawerButton ||
      drawer.dataset.mobileNavInitialized === "true"
    ) {
      return;
    }

    const navTabElements = Array.from(
      drawer.querySelectorAll("[data-mobile-nav-tab]")
    );
    const defaultSearchPlaceholder =
      drawer.dataset.defaultSearchPlaceholder || "Search the site";
    const defaultSearchScope = drawer.dataset.defaultSearchScope || "";
    const headerSearchOverlay = document.getElementById(
      "header-search-overlay"
    );
    const navLinkElements = Array.from(
      drawer.querySelectorAll("[data-mobile-nav-link]")
    );
    const tabPanels = Array.from(
      drawer.querySelectorAll("[data-mobile-nav-content]")
    );
    const isStarlightApiReferenceRoute =
      window.location.pathname === "/api/reference" ||
      window.location.pathname.startsWith("/api/reference/");
    const shouldRestoreDrawerOpen =
      matchMedia("(max-width: 50rem)").matches &&
      !isStarlightApiReferenceRoute &&
      readPersistedMobileNavOpen();

    let activeTabId =
      drawer.dataset.defaultTabId ||
      navTabElements.find((tab) => tab.dataset.selected === "true")?.dataset
        .tabId ||
      null;

    const updateSelectedOption = (tabId) => {
      let selectedLabel = "";
      let selectedPlaceholder = "";
      let selectedScope = "";

      navTabElements.forEach((tab) => {
        const isSelected = tab.dataset.tabId === tabId;
        tab.dataset.selected = isSelected ? "true" : "false";
        tab.setAttribute("aria-selected", isSelected ? "true" : "false");

        if (isSelected && !selectedLabel) {
          selectedLabel = tab.dataset.label || tab.textContent?.trim() || "";
        }

        if (isSelected && !selectedPlaceholder) {
          selectedPlaceholder = tab.dataset.searchPlaceholder || "";
        }

        if (isSelected && !selectedScope) {
          selectedScope = tab.dataset.searchScope || "";
        }
      });

      if (!selectedLabel && navTabElements[0]) {
        selectedLabel =
          navTabElements[0].dataset.label ||
          navTabElements[0].textContent?.trim() ||
          "";
      }

      if (!selectedPlaceholder && navTabElements[0]) {
        selectedPlaceholder = navTabElements[0].dataset.searchPlaceholder || "";
      }

      if (!selectedScope && navTabElements[0]) {
        selectedScope = navTabElements[0].dataset.searchScope || "";
      }

      const nextPlaceholder = selectedPlaceholder || defaultSearchPlaceholder;
      const nextScope = selectedScope || defaultSearchScope;
      const updatePlaceholder = (container) => {
        if (!container) return;
        const input = container.querySelector("[data-site-search-input]");
        if (input instanceof HTMLInputElement) {
          input.placeholder = nextPlaceholder;
        }
      };
      const updateScope = (container) => {
        if (!container) return;
        const target = container.querySelector("[data-site-search-root]");
        if (!target) return;
        target.setAttribute("data-scope", nextScope);
        target.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("site-search:update"));
      };
      updatePlaceholder(drawer);
      updatePlaceholder(headerSearchOverlay);
      updateScope(drawer);
      updateScope(headerSearchOverlay);
    };

    const activeVariantByTabId = new Map();

    const getTabLabel = (tabId) => {
      return (
        navTabElements.find((tab) => tab.dataset.tabId === tabId)?.dataset
          .label || ""
      );
    };

    const updatePanelBreadcrumb = (panel, tabId, contextLabel) => {
      const breadcrumb = panel.querySelector("[data-mobile-breadcrumb]");
      const parent = panel.querySelector("[data-mobile-breadcrumb-parent]");
      const childWrapper = panel.querySelector(
        "[data-mobile-breadcrumb-child-wrapper]"
      );
      const child = panel.querySelector("[data-mobile-breadcrumb-child]");
      const contextOptions = panel.querySelector(
        "[data-mobile-context-options]"
      );

      if (contextOptions) {
        contextOptions.dataset.contextActive = contextLabel ? "true" : "false";
      }

      if (!breadcrumb || !parent || !childWrapper || !child) {
        return;
      }

      const tabLabel = getTabLabel(tabId);
      parent.textContent = tabLabel;

      if (!contextLabel) {
        breadcrumb.setAttribute("hidden", "true");
        childWrapper.setAttribute("hidden", "true");
        child.textContent = "";
        return;
      }

      breadcrumb.removeAttribute("hidden");
      childWrapper.removeAttribute("hidden");
      child.textContent = contextLabel;
    };

    const selectVariantForPanel = (panel, tabId, variantId) => {
      if (!variantId) {
        updatePanelBreadcrumb(panel, tabId, "");
        return;
      }

      const contextOptions = Array.from(
        panel.querySelectorAll("[data-mobile-context-option]")
      );
      let selectedContextLabel = "";

      contextOptions.forEach((option) => {
        const isSelected = option.dataset.contextId === variantId;
        option.dataset.selected = isSelected ? "true" : "false";
        if (isSelected) {
          selectedContextLabel = option.dataset.contextLabel || "";
        }
      });

      const variantSections = Array.from(
        panel.querySelectorAll("[data-mobile-nav-variant-content]")
      );
      variantSections.forEach((section) => {
        const isSelected = section.dataset.variantId === variantId;
        if (isSelected) {
          section.removeAttribute("hidden");
        } else {
          section.setAttribute("hidden", "true");
        }
      });

      updatePanelBreadcrumb(panel, tabId, selectedContextLabel);
      activeVariantByTabId.set(tabId, variantId);
    };

    const activateTab = (tabId) => {
      if (!tabId) return;
      activeTabId = tabId;
      updateSelectedOption(tabId);

      tabPanels.forEach((panel) => {
        const panelTabId = panel.getAttribute("data-tab-id");
        const isActive = panelTabId === tabId;
        if (isActive) {
          panel.removeAttribute("hidden");
          const defaultVariantId = panel.getAttribute(
            "data-default-variant-id"
          );
          const nextVariantId =
            activeVariantByTabId.get(tabId) ||
            defaultVariantId ||
            panel.querySelector("[data-mobile-nav-variant-content]")?.dataset
              .variantId ||
            "";
          selectVariantForPanel(panel, tabId, nextVariantId);
        } else {
          panel.setAttribute("hidden", "true");
        }
      });
    };

    const closeDrawer = () => {
      drawer.classList.remove("open");
      drawerButton.classList.remove("open");
      drawerButton.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
      setPersistedMobileNavOpen(false);
    };

    const openDrawer = () => {
      drawer.classList.add("open");
      drawerButton.classList.add("open");
      drawerButton.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
      if (activeTabId) {
        activateTab(activeTabId);
      }
    };

    const toggleDrawer = () => {
      if (drawer.classList.contains("open")) {
        closeDrawer();
      } else {
        openDrawer();
      }
    };

    const handleTabSelection = (tab) => {
      const hasNav = tab.dataset.hasNav === "true";
      const href = tab.dataset.href;
      const tabId = tab.dataset.tabId;

      if (!tabId) {
        return;
      }

      if (!hasNav && href) {
        setPersistedMobileNavOpen(true);
        window.location.href = href;
        return;
      }

      activateTab(tabId);
    };

    drawerButton.addEventListener("click", toggleDrawer);

    navTabElements.forEach((tab) => {
      tab.addEventListener("click", () => {
        handleTabSelection(tab);
      });

      tab.addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
        if (!navTabElements.length) return;

        const currentIndex = navTabElements.indexOf(tab);

        if (event.key === "ArrowRight") {
          event.preventDefault();
          const nextIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % navTabElements.length;
          navTabElements[nextIndex]?.focus();
        } else if (event.key === "ArrowLeft") {
          event.preventDefault();
          const prevIndex =
            (currentIndex - 1 + navTabElements.length) % navTabElements.length;
          navTabElements[prevIndex]?.focus();
        } else if (event.key === "Home") {
          event.preventDefault();
          navTabElements[0]?.focus();
        } else if (event.key === "End") {
          event.preventDefault();
          navTabElements[navTabElements.length - 1]?.focus();
        } else if (
          event.key === "Enter" ||
          event.key === " " ||
          event.key === "Space" ||
          event.key === "Spacebar"
        ) {
          event.preventDefault();
          handleTabSelection(tab);
        } else if (event.key === "Escape") {
          event.preventDefault();
          closeDrawer();
          drawerButton.focus();
        }
      });
    });

    tabPanels.forEach((panel) => {
      const tabId = panel.getAttribute("data-tab-id") || "";
      const contextOptions = Array.from(
        panel.querySelectorAll("[data-mobile-context-option]")
      );

      contextOptions.forEach((option) => {
        option.addEventListener("click", () => {
          const contextHref = option.dataset.contextHref;
          if (
            contextHref &&
            contextHref.startsWith("/api/reference") &&
            tabId
          ) {
            closeDrawer();
            window.location.href = contextHref;
            return;
          }

          const variantId = option.dataset.contextId;
          if (!variantId || !tabId) {
            return;
          }

          selectVariantForPanel(panel, tabId, variantId);
        });
      });
    });

    navLinkElements.forEach((link) => {
      link.addEventListener("click", () => {
        closeDrawer();
      });
    });

    const mobileSearch = drawer.querySelector("[data-mobile-search]");
    mobileSearch?.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      const target = event.target;
      if (target instanceof Element) {
        const anchor = target.closest("a[href]");
        if (anchor) {
          closeDrawer();
        }
      }
    });

    mobileSearch?.addEventListener("focusin", (event) => {
      const target = event.target;
      if (!(target instanceof HTMLInputElement) || target.type !== "text") {
        return;
      }
      closeDrawer();
      window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        if (document.activeElement === target) {
          target.blur();
        }
        document.dispatchEvent(
          new CustomEvent("header:open-search", {
            detail: {
              trigger: target,
              variant: "mobile",
            },
          })
        );
      });
    });

    drawer.addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
      if (event.key === "Escape") {
        closeDrawer();
        drawerButton.focus();
      }
    });

    drawer.dataset.mobileNavInitialized = "true";
    if (activeTabId) {
      activateTab(activeTabId);
    }

    if (shouldRestoreDrawerOpen) {
      openDrawer();
      setPersistedMobileNavOpen(false);
    }
  }

  function initializeHeaderSearch() {
    const overlay = document.getElementById("header-search-overlay");
    if (!overlay) {
      return;
    }

    const getSearchButtons = () =>
      Array.from(document.querySelectorAll("[data-header-search-button]"));

    const closeButtons = overlay.querySelectorAll("[data-header-search-close]");
    const dismissTarget = overlay.querySelector("[data-header-search-dismiss]");
    const panel = overlay.querySelector("[data-header-search-panel]");
    const overlayMobileClass = "header-search-overlay--mobile";
    const panelMobileClass = "header-search-panel--mobile";
    let lastTrigger = null;
    let lastVariant = null;

    const setExpandedState = (isOpen) => {
      const expanded = isOpen ? "true" : "false";
      getSearchButtons().forEach((button) => {
        button.setAttribute("aria-expanded", expanded);
        button.setAttribute("data-active", expanded);
      });
      overlay.dataset.open = expanded;
      overlay.setAttribute("aria-hidden", isOpen ? "false" : "true");
    };

    const focusSearchInput = () => {
      window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        const input = overlay.querySelector("[data-site-search-input]");
        if (input) {
          input.focus();
          input.select();
        }
      });
    };

    const openOverlay = (trigger, options = {}) => {
      lastTrigger = trigger ?? document.activeElement;
      const variant = options.variant ?? null;
      lastVariant = typeof variant === "string" ? variant : null;
      overlay.classList.remove("hidden");
      overlay.classList.add("flex");
      const isMobileVariant = lastVariant === "mobile";
      if (isMobileVariant) {
        overlay.dataset.variant = "mobile";
      } else {
        delete overlay.dataset.variant;
      }
      overlay.classList.toggle(overlayMobileClass, isMobileVariant);
      panel?.classList.toggle(panelMobileClass, isMobileVariant);
      document.documentElement.classList.add("has-header-search-open");
      setExpandedState(true);
      focusSearchInput();
    };

    const closeOverlay = () => {
      overlay.classList.add("hidden");
      overlay.classList.remove("flex");
      document.documentElement.classList.remove("has-header-search-open");
      overlay.classList.remove(overlayMobileClass);
      panel?.classList.remove(panelMobileClass);
      delete overlay.dataset.variant;
      setExpandedState(false);
      if (lastTrigger instanceof HTMLElement) {
        if (
          lastVariant === "mobile" &&
          typeof lastTrigger.blur === "function"
        ) {
          lastTrigger.blur();
        } else if (lastVariant !== "mobile") {
          lastTrigger.focus();
        }
      }
      lastTrigger = null;
      lastVariant = null;
    };

    const bindSearchButtons = () => {
      getSearchButtons().forEach((button) => {
        if (button.dataset.searchButtonInitialized === "true") {
          return;
        }

        button.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
          event.preventDefault();
          openOverlay(button);
        });

        button.dataset.searchButtonInitialized = "true";
      });
    };

    if (overlay.dataset.searchInitialized !== "true") {
      closeButtons.forEach((button) => {
        button.addEventListener("click", () => {
          closeOverlay();
        });
      });

      overlay.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
        if (event.target === overlay) {
          closeOverlay();
        }
      });

      dismissTarget?.addEventListener("click", closeOverlay);

      const handleKeydown = (event) => {
        const key = "key" in event ? event.key : undefined;
        const isShortcut =
          !!key &&
          key.toLowerCase() === "k" &&
          (event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey);

        if (isShortcut) {
          event.preventDefault();
          const buttons = getSearchButtons();
          openOverlay(buttons[0] ?? null);
          return;
        }

        if (key === "Escape" && overlay.dataset.open === "true") {
          event.preventDefault();
          closeOverlay();
        }
      };

      document.addEventListener("keydown", handleKeydown);

      document.addEventListener("header:open-search", (event) => {
        const detail =
          event instanceof CustomEvent && typeof event.detail === "object"
            ? event.detail
            : {};
        const trigger =
          detail && detail.trigger instanceof HTMLElement
            ? detail.trigger
            : null;
        openOverlay(trigger, detail);
      });

      document.addEventListener("astro:before-swap", () => {
        if (overlay.dataset.open === "true") {
          closeOverlay();
        }
      });

      overlay.dataset.searchInitialized = "true";
    }

    bindSearchButtons();
  }

  const handleAfterSwap = () => {
    initializeMobileNavigation();
    window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      initializeHeaderSearch();
    });
  };

  document.addEventListener("astro:after-swap", handleAfterSwap);
  handleAfterSwap();
</script> <div class="flex pt-16"> <div class="hidden md:flex md:flex-col w-[218px] px-3 pb-6 pt-2 md:fixed md:top-16 md:bottom-0 md:z-40 bg-surface dark:bg-black astro-73gi4scu"   const NAV_SELECTOR = "nav[data-left-nav]";
  const STORAGE_PREFIX = "left-nav-scroll:";
  const INITIALIZED_ATTRIBUTE = "data-left-nav-scroll-initialized";

  const isStorageAvailable = (() => {
    try {
      const storageKey = `${STORAGE_PREFIX}__test__`;
      sessionStorage.setItem(storageKey, "1");
      sessionStorage.removeItem(storageKey);
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      return false;
    }
  })();

  const getNav = () => document.querySelector(NAV_SELECTOR);

  const getStorageKey = (nav) =>
    `${STORAGE_PREFIX}${nav.dataset.leftNavId ?? "default"}`;

  const restoreScrollPosition = (nav) => {
    if (!isStorageAvailable) return;
    const storedValue = sessionStorage.getItem(getStorageKey(nav));
    if (storedValue !== null) {
      nav.scrollTop = Number(storedValue);
    }
  };

  const saveScrollPosition = (nav) => {
    if (!isStorageAvailable) return;
    sessionStorage.setItem(getStorageKey(nav), String(nav.scrollTop));
  };

  const setupNav = () => {
    const nav = getNav();
    if (!nav || nav.getAttribute(INITIALIZED_ATTRIBUTE) === "true") return;

    restoreScrollPosition(nav);

    nav.addEventListener(
      "scroll",
      () => {
        saveScrollPosition(nav);
      },
      { passive: true }
    );

    nav.setAttribute(INITIALIZED_ATTRIBUTE, "true");
  };

  const persistScrollPosition = () => {
    const nav = getNav();
    if (!nav) return;
    saveScrollPosition(nav);
  };

  const initialize = () => {
    setupNav();
    const nav = getNav();
    if (!nav) return;
    restoreScrollPosition(nav);
  };

  window.addEventListener("pageshow", initialize);
  document.addEventListener("astro:page-load", initialize);
  document.addEventListener("astro:after-swap", initialize);

  document.addEventListener("astro:before-swap", persistScrollPosition);
  window.addEventListener("beforeunload", persistScrollPosition);

  initialize();
</script> <main class="min-w-0 flex-1 md:pl-[240px]">  <div class="page-container md:max-w-6xl pb-12 pt-0"> <div class="mx-auto md:w-full grid grid-cols-1 gap-12 max-w-7xl <h2 id="the-shift-in-mindset" class="group flex items-center gap-2 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">The Shift in Mindset</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center <p>Every enterprise faces the same tension: the pressure to adopt AI is immense, but so is the fear of getting it wrong. Teams want to build, legal wants to review, security wants to audit, and promising pilots stall because no one can answer: <em>“Is this safe to deploy?”</em></p>
<p>Organizations have moved past <em>“Should we experiment with AI?”</em> and now ask <em>“How do we get this into production safely?”</em> The prototypes worked, the demos impressed the board, and now there’s real pressure to deliver AI that touches real customers and handles real data. But production demands answers that pilots never required: What happens when it fails? Who’s accountable? How do we prove it’s compliant?</p>
<p>The organizations winning at AI have discovered something counterintuitive: <strong>governance drives delivery.</strong> When guardrails are clear and automated, teams build with confidence. When policies travel with the code, security reviews become approvals instead of interrogations. When compliance is infrastructure rather than inspection, pilots graduate to production in weeks, not quarters.</p>
<p>The goal is to build the scaffolding that lets you move fast <em>because</em> you’re safe.</p>

self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info focus-visible:opacity-100 motion-reduce:transition-none relative -top-0.5" data-anchor-id="what-this-cookbook-delivers" aria-label="Copy link to What This Cookbook Delivers" title="Copy link to What This Cookbook Delivers"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" aria-hidden="true" class="h-3.5 w-3.5"><path d="M18.2929 5.7071C16.4743 3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 11.7071 5.7071L10.7071 6.7071C10.3166 7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 9.29289 6.7071C8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 5.68341 9.29289 5.29289L10.2929 4.29289C12.8926 1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 19.7071 4.29289C22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 11.1074 19.7071 13.7071L18.7071 14.7071C18.3166 15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 17.2929 14.7071C16.9024 14.3166 16.9024 13.6834 17.2929 13.2929L18.2929 12.2929C20.1115 10.4743 20.1115 7.52572 19.7071C1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 12.8926 4.29289 10.2929L5.29289 9.29289C5.68341 8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 6.7071 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>This guide shows you how to make governance part of core infrastructure from day one, instead of a launch-time afterthought.</p>
<p>You’ll learn to:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Define policies as code</strong> that version, travel, and deploy alongside your applications</li>
<li><strong>Apply guardrails automatically</strong> to every AI call - no manual review bottlenecks</li>
<li><strong>Evaluate your defenses</strong> with precision and recall metrics, so you know they actually work</li>
<li><strong>Package governance for distribution</strong> so any team can <code>pip install</code> instant compliance</li>
<li><strong>Build agentic systems</strong> with proper handoffs, observability, and oversight from day one</li>
</ul>
<p>Each section pairs a concrete governance objective with a practical implementation pattern, including example configurations, code snippets, and integration points you can adapt to your own environment.</p>
<p>By the end, you’ll have a working blueprint for governed AI that scales across your organization and turns governance from a friction point into a competitive advantage.</p>
<hr>
<h2 id="what-well-build" class="group flex items-center gap-2 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">What We’ll Build</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" aria-hidden="true" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M18.2929 5.7071C16.4743 3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 11.7071 5.7071L10.7071 6.7071C10.3166 7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 9.29289 9.29289C5.68341 8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 6.7071 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h2>
<p>We’ll create a <strong>Private Equity firm AI assistant</strong> with:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Multiple specialist agents</strong> that handle different domains</li>
<li><strong>A triage agent</strong> that routes queries via handoffs</li>
<li><strong>Built-in guardrails</strong> that validate queries before processing</li>
<li><strong>Tracing</strong> for full observability of agent behavior</li>
<li><strong>Centralized policy enforcement</strong> via an installable package</li>
<li><strong>Eval-driven</strong> system design for reliability &#x26; scalability</li>
</ol>
<p>The architecture looks like this:</p>
<p><img src="/cookbook/assets/images/01_alti_agent_governance.png" alt="PE Agent Architecture"></p>
<p>The pipeline treats red team (adversarial) inputs the same way as user queries: they flow through pre-flight, input guardrails, orchestration, and output guardrails. GuardrailEval and the feedback loop use results from both normal and adversarial runs to tune policy and harden defenses.</p>

<p>Before we begin, you’ll need:</p>
<ul>
<li>Python 3.9+</li>
<li>An OpenAI API key</li>
<li>A GitHub account (for the policy repo)</li>

<p>In this section we’ll build a PE firm AI assistant from scratch: define tools, create specialist agents, and wire up handoffs between them.</p>
<h3 id="understanding-agents-and-tools" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Understanding Agents and Tools</span><button type="button" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>An <strong>agent</strong> is an AI system that can:</p>
<ul>
<li>Receive instructions that define its role and behavior</li>
<li>Use <strong>tools</strong> to take actions (search databases, create records, call APIs)</li>
<li><strong>Hand off</strong> to other agents when a task is outside its expertise</li>
<li>Maintain context across a conversation</li>
</ul>
<p>Think of agents like employees with specific job descriptions. A receptionist (triage agent) knows who to route calls to, while specialists (domain agents) have deep expertise in specific areas.</p>
<h3 id="why-use-tools" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Why Use Tools?</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex 9.29289C5.68341 8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 6.7071 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>Tools extend what agents can do beyond just generating text:</p>





















<table><thead><tr><th>Without Tools</th><th>With Tools</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>”I can tell you about deal evaluation best practices"</td><td>"Let me search your deal database… Found 3 matches"</td></tr><tr><td>"You should check your portfolio metrics"</td><td>"Acme Corp: Revenue $50M (+15% YoY), EBITDA $8M"</td></tr><tr><td>"Consider creating a deal memo"</td><td>"Deal memo created for TechCorp in your system”</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><strong>Important</strong>: OpenAI doesn’t execute tools for you - it tells your application which tools to call and with what parameters. Your code executes the actual logic.</p>

19.7071C1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 12.8926 4.29289 10.2929L5.29289 9.29289C5.68341 8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 6.7071 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>Tools are Python functions decorated with <code>@function_tool</code>. The docstring becomes the tool’s description that the agent sees.</p>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="python"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> agents </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> function_tool</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">@function_tool</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">def</span><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> search_deal_database</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(query: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">str</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) -> </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">str</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    """Search the deal pipeline database for companies or opportunities.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    Use this when the user asks about potential investments, deal flow,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    or wants to find companies matching certain criteria.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    # In production: connect to your CRM/deal tracking system</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Found 3 matches for '</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">query</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">': TechCorp (Series B), HealthCo (Growth), DataInc (Buyout)"</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">@function_tool</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">def</span><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> get_portfolio_metrics</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(company_name: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">str</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) -> </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">str</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    """Retrieve key metrics for a portfolio company.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    Use this when the user asks about performance, KPIs, or financials</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    for a company we've already invested in.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    # In production: pull from your portfolio monitoring system</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">company_name</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> metrics: Revenue $50M (+15% YoY), EBITDA $8M, ARR Growth 22%"</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">@function_tool</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">def</span><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> create_deal_memo</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(company_name: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">str</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, summary: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">str</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) -> </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">str</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    """Create a new deal memo entry in the system.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    Use this when the user wants to document initial thoughts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    or findings about a potential investment.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    # In production: integrate with your document management</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Deal memo created for </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">company_name</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">summary</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Tools defined:"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">" - search_deal_database: Find investment opportunities"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">" - get_portfolio_metrics: Get portfolio company KPIs"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">" - create_deal_memo: Document deal findings"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span></code></pre>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="text"><code><span class="line"><span>Tools defined:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span> - search_deal_database: Find investment opportunities</span></span>
<span class="line"><span> - get_portfolio_metrics: Get portfolio company KPIs</span></span>
<span class="line"><span> - create_deal_memo: Document deal findings</span></span></code></pre>
<hr>
<h3 id="multi-agent-system-with-handoffs" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Multi-Agent System with Handoffs</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info focus-visible:opacity-100 group-focus-within:opacity-100 focus-visible:outline focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-gray-300 group-hover:opacity-100 dark:focus-visible:outline-gray-600 motion-reduce:transition-none relative -top-0.5" data-anchor-id="multi-agent-system-with-handoffs" aria-label="Copy link to Multi-Agent System with Handoffs" title="Copy link to Multi-Agent System with Handoffs"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" aria-hidden="true" class="h-3.5 w-3.5"><path d="M18.2929 5.7071C16.4743 3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 11.7071 5.7071L10.7071 6.7071C10.3166 7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 9.29289 6.7071C8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 5.68341 9.29289 5.29289L10.2929 4.29289C12.8926 1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 19.7071 4.29289C22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 11.1074 19.7071 13.7071L18.7071 14.7071C18.3166 15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 17.2929 14.7071C16.9024 14.3166 16.9024 13.6834 17.2929 13.2929L18.2929 12.2929C20.1115 10.4743 20.1115 7.52572 18.2929 5.7071ZM15.7071 8.29289C16.0976 8.68341 16.0976 9.31658 15.7071 9.7071L9.7071 15.7071C9.31658 16.0976 8.68341 16.0976 8.29289 15.7071C7.90236 15.3166 7.90236 14.6834 8.29289 14.2929L14.2929 8.29289C14.6834 7.90236 15.3166 7.90236 15.7071 8.29289ZM6.7071 9.29289C7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 10.3166 6.7071 10.7071L5.7071 11.7071C3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 16.4743 5.7071 18.2929C7.52572 20.1115 10.4743 20.1115 12.2929 18.2929L13.2929 17.2929C13.6834 16.9024 14.3166 16.9024 14.7071 17.2929C15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 18.3166 14.7071 18.7071L13.7071 19.7071C11.1074 22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 4.29289 19.7071C1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 12.8926 4.29289 10.2929L5.29289 9.29289C5.68341 8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 6.7071 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>Real-world tasks rarely fit into a single agent’s expertise. Consider a PE firm:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Deal questions</strong> need investment criteria knowledge</li>
<li><strong>Portfolio questions</strong> need operational metrics expertise</li>
<li><strong>LP questions</strong> need compliance awareness and fund knowledge</li>
</ul>
<p>You could build one massive agent with all this knowledge, but instructions become unwieldy, the agent struggles to stay “in character”, and you can’t easily update one domain without affecting others.</p>
<p><strong>Handoffs</strong> solve this by letting agents delegate to specialists:</p>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="plaintext"><code><span class="line"><span>User: "What's our IRR on Fund II?"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    │</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    ▼</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>Triage Agent: "This is an LP/investor question"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    │</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    ▼ (handoff)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>IR Agent: "Fund II IRR is 22.5% net as of Q3..."</span></span></code></pre>
<p>The user sees one seamless conversation, but behind the scenes, the right expert is answering.</p>
<h3 id="step-2-create-specialist-agents" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Step 2: Create Specialist Agents</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info focus-visible:opacity-100 group-focus-within:opacity-100 focus-visible:outline focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-gray-300 group-hover:opacity-100 dark:focus-visible:outline-gray-600 motion-reduce:transition-none relative -top-0.5" data-anchor-id="step-2-create-specialist-agents" aria-label="Copy link to Step 2: Create Specialist Agents" title="Copy link to Step 2: Create Specialist Agents"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" aria-hidden="true" class="h-3.5 w-3.5"><path d="M18.2929 5.7071C16.4743 3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 11.7071 5.7071L10.7071 6.7071C10.3166 7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 9.29289 6.7071C8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 5.68341 9.29289 5.29289L10.2929 4.29289C12.8926 1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 19.7071 4.29289C22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 11.1074 19.7071 13.7071L18.7071 14.7071C18.3166 15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 17.2929 14.7071C16.9024 14.3166 16.9024 13.6834 17.2929 13.2929L18.2929 12.2929C20.1115 10.4743 20.1115 7.52572 18.2929 5.7071ZM15.7071 8.29289C16.0976 8.68341 16.0976 9.31658 15.7071 9.7071L9.7071 15.7071C9.31658 16.0976 8.68341 16.0976 8.29289 15.7071C7.90236 15.3166 7.90236 14.6834 8.29289 14.2929L14.2929 8.29289C14.6834 7.90236 15.3166 7.90236 15.7071 8.29289ZM6.7071 9.29289C7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 10.3166 6.7071 10.7071L5.7071 11.7071C3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 16.4743 5.7071 18.2929C7.52572 20.1115 10.4743 20.1115 12.2929 18.2929L13.2929 17.2929C13.6834 16.9024 14.3166 16.9024 14.7071 17.2929C15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 18.3166 14.7071 18.7071L13.7071 19.7071C11.1074 22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 4.29289 19.7071C1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 12.8926 4.29289 10.2929L5.29289 9.29289C5.68341 8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 6.7071 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>Each specialist has:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>name</strong>: Identifier for the agent</li>
<li><strong>handoff_description</strong>: Tells the triage agent WHEN to route here (critical!)</li>
<li><strong>instructions</strong>: Defines HOW the agent should behave</li>
</ul>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="python"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> agents </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Agent</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Deal Screening Specialist</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">deal_screening_agent </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Agent(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    name</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"DealScreeningAgent"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    model</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"gpt-5.2"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    # This description is what the triage agent sees to decide on handoffs</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    handoff_description</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Handles deal sourcing, screening, and initial evaluation of investment opportunities. Route here for questions about potential acquisitions, investment criteria, or target company analysis."</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    instructions</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "You are a deal screening specialist at a Private Equity firm. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "Help evaluate potential investment opportunities, assess fit with investment criteria, "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "and provide initial analysis on target companies. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "Focus on: industry dynamics, company size, growth trajectory, margin profile, and competitive positioning. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "Always ask clarifying questions about investment thesis if unclear."</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Portfolio Management Specialist</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">portfolio_agent </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Agent(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    name</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"PortfolioAgent"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    model</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"gpt-5.2"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    handoff_description</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Handles questions about existing portfolio companies and their performance. Route here for questions about companies we've already invested in, operational improvements, or exit planning."</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    instructions</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "You are a portfolio management specialist at a Private Equity firm. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "Help with questions about portfolio company performance, value creation initiatives, "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "operational improvements, and exit planning. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "You have access to portfolio metrics and can retrieve KPIs for any portfolio company."</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Investor Relations Specialist</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">investor_relations_agent </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Agent(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    name</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"InvestorRelationsAgent"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    model</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"gpt-5.2"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    handoff_description</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Handles LP inquiries, fund performance questions, and capital calls. Route here for questions from or about Limited Partners, fund returns, distributions, or reporting."</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    instructions</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "You are an investor relations specialist at a Private Equity firm. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "Help with LP (Limited Partner) inquiries about fund performance, distributions, "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "capital calls, and reporting. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "Be professional, compliance-aware, and never share confidential LP information. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "If asked about specific LP details, explain that such information is confidential."</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Specialist agents created:"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">for</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> agent </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">in</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [deal_screening_agent, portfolio_agent, investor_relations_agent]:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  {</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">agent.name</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">:"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"    Routes when: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">agent.handoff_description[:</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">80</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">]</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">..."</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span></code></pre>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="text"><code><span class="line"><span>Specialist agents created:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>

<span class="line"><span>    Routes when: Handles deal sourcing, screening, and initial evaluation of investment opportuni...</span></span>

<span class="line"><span>  PortfolioAgent:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    Routes when: Handles questions about existing portfolio companies and their performance. Rout...</span></span>

<span class="line"><span>    Routes when: Handles LP inquiries, fund performance questions, and capital calls. Route here ...</span></span></code></pre>

fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>The triage agent is the “front door”. It:</p>
<ol>
<li>Receives all incoming queries</li>
<li>Decides which specialist should handle it (using <code>handoff_description</code>)</li>
<li>Hands off the conversation seamlessly</li>
</ol>
<p>The <code>handoffs</code> parameter tells the agent which specialists it can delegate to.</p>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="python"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">pe_concierge </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Agent(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    name</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"PEConcierge"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    model</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"gpt-5.2"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    instructions</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "You are the front-desk assistant for a Private Equity firm. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "Your job is to understand incoming queries and route them to the right specialist. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n\n</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">Routing guidelines:"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">- Deal/investment/acquisition questions → DealScreeningAgent"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">- Portfolio company performance/operations → PortfolioAgent"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">- LP/investor/fund performance questions → InvestorRelationsAgent"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n\n</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">If a query is ambiguous, ask ONE clarifying question before routing. "</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "If a query is clearly off-topic (not PE-related), politely explain what you can help with."</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    # These are the agents we can hand off to</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    handoffs</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">[deal_screening_agent, portfolio_agent, investor_relations_agent],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    # Tools available to the triage agent (optional - specialists could have their own)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    tools</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">[search_deal_database, get_portfolio_metrics, create_deal_memo],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Triage agent '</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">pe_concierge.name</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">' created"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"  Can hand off to: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">[a.name </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">for</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> a </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">in</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> pe_concierge.handoffs]</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"  Has tools: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">[t.name </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">for</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> t </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">in</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> pe_concierge.tools]</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span></code></pre>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="text"><code><span class="line"><span>Triage agent 'PEConcierge' created</span></span>

<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="python"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> pprint</span></span>

<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="text"><code><span class="line"><span>════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>TEST 1: Deal Screening Query</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>Response: Evaluate it like a classic PE diligence funnel—market, product, unit economics, and “quality of revenue”—but tailored to healthcare IT (regulatory + workflow + integrations + reimbursement). Below is a practical checklist for a $30M-revenue mid-market target, plus the key questions I’d want answered to refine the investment thesis.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>## 1) Industry / market dynamics (healthcare IT-specific)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>- **End-market segment**: Provider (hospitals, IDNs, ambulatory, post-acute), payer, life sciences, dental,...</span></span></code></pre>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="python"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Test: Portfolio query (should hand off to PortfolioAgent)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"═"</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> *</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> 60</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"TEST 2: Portfolio Query"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"═"</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> *</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> 60</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">result </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Runner.run(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    pe_concierge, </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    "How is Acme Corp performing this quarter? Are we on track for the exit?"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>

<h3 id="tracing---observability-for-agents" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Tracing - Observability for Agents</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info focus-visible:opacity-100 group-focus-within:opacity-100 focus-visible:outline focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-gray-300 group-hover:opacity-100 dark:focus-visible:outline-gray-600 motion-reduce:transition-none relative -top-0.5" data-anchor-id="tracing---observability-for-agents" aria-label="Copy link to Tracing - <p>With multi-agent systems, a single user query can trigger multiple LLM calls, tool executions, handoffs between agents, and guardrail checks. <strong>Tracing</strong> captures all of this in a structured way, giving you:</p>

























<table><thead><tr><th>Benefit</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><strong>Debugging</strong></td><td>See exactly what happened when something goes wrong</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Performance</strong></td><td>Identify slow steps in your agent workflows</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Auditing</strong></td><td>Review what agents did and why</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Optimization</strong></td><td>Find opportunities to improve prompts or reduce calls</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3 id="using-the-trace-context-manager" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Using the <code>trace()</code> Context Manager</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info focus-visible:opacity-100 group-focus-within:opacity-100 focus-visible:outline focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-gray-300 group-hover:opacity-100 title="Copy link to Using the trace() Context Manager"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" aria-hidden="true" class="h-3.5 w-3.5"><path d="M18.2929 5.7071C16.4743 3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 11.7071 5.7071L10.7071 6.7071C10.3166 7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 9.29289 6.7071C8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 5.68341 9.29289 5.29289L10.2929 4.29289C12.8926 <p>The <code>trace()</code> function wraps operations under a named trace, linking all spans together. After running, you can view the complete trace - including every LLM call, tool execution, and handoff - in the <strong>OpenAI Traces Dashboard</strong>.</p>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="python"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> agents </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> trace</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># The trace() context manager groups all operations under a single trace ID</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># This links together: LLM calls, tool executions, handoffs, and guardrail checks</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">with</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> trace(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"PE Deal Inquiry"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    result </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Runner.run(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        pe_concierge,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">        "Find me SaaS companies in the deal pipeline with over $20M ARR"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Response: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">result.final_output[:</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">300</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">]</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">..."</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># View your trace in the OpenAI dashboard - you'll see the full execution flow:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Agent reasoning → Tool calls → Responses → Handoffs (if any)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">✓ Trace captured! View it at: https://platform.openai.com/traces"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span></code></pre>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="text"><code><span class="line"><span>Response: These SaaS companies in our deal pipeline show **>$20M ARR**:</span></span>

<h3 id="trace-naming-best-practices" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Trace Naming Best Practices</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 <p>Good trace names help you find and analyze specific workflows:</p>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="python"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># ❌ Bad: Generic names</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">with</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> trace(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"query"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    ...</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># ✅ Good: Descriptive, searchable names</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">with</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> trace(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Deal Screening - Healthcare"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    ...</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">with</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> trace(</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"LP Inquiry - </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">lp_name</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    ...</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">with</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> trace(</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Portfolio Review - </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">company</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> - Q</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">quarter</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    ...</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="tracing-for-compliant-industries-zero-data-retention" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Tracing for Compliant Industries (Zero Data Retention)</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info focus-visible:opacity-100 group-focus-within:opacity-100 focus-visible:outline focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-gray-300 to Tracing for Compliant Industries (Zero Data Retention)" title="Copy link to Tracing for Compliant Industries (Zero Data Retention)"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" aria-hidden="true" class="h-3.5 w-3.5"><path d="M18.2929 5.7071C16.4743 3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 11.7071 5.7071L10.7071 6.7071C10.3166 7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 9.29289 14.3166 16.9024 14.7071 17.2929C15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 18.3166 14.7071 18.7071L13.7071 19.7071C11.1074 22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 4.29289 19.7071C1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 12.8926 4.29289 10.2929L5.29289 9.29289C5.68341 8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 6.7071 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>Some organizations have <strong>Zero Data Retention (ZDR)</strong> agreements with OpenAI, meaning:</p>
<ul>
<li>Data is not stored or retained after processing</li>
<li>The built-in tracing dashboard <strong>cannot be used</strong> (it stores traces in OpenAI’s systems)</li>
</ul>
<p>This is common in financial services, healthcare (HIPAA), government, and organizations with strict data residency rules.</p>

























<table><thead><tr><th>Org Type</th><th>Built-in Dashboard</th><th>What to Do</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><strong>Non-ZDR</strong></td><td>✅ Allowed</td><td>Use default tracing; view traces in dashboard</td></tr><tr><td><strong>ZDR (strict)</strong></td><td>❌ Not allowed</td><td>Disable tracing entirely</td></tr><tr><td><strong>ZDR (needs observability)</strong></td><td>❌ Not allowed</td><td>Use trace processors to stream to your internal systems</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3 id="option-1-disable-tracing-entirely" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Option 1: Disable Tracing Entirely</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info d="M18.2929 5.7071C16.4743 3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 11.7071 5.7071L10.7071 6.7071C10.3166 7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 9.29289 6.7071C8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 5.68341 9.29289 5.29289L10.2929 4.29289C12.8926 1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 19.7071 4.29289C22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 11.1074 19.7071 13.7071L18.7071 14.7071C18.3166 15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 17.2929 14.7071C16.9024 14.3166 16.9024 13.6834 17.2929 15.7071C7.90236 15.3166 7.90236 14.6834 8.29289 14.2929L14.2929 8.29289C14.6834 7.90236 15.3166 7.90236 15.7071 8.29289ZM6.7071 9.29289C7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 10.3166 6.7071 10.7071L5.7071 fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>For strict ZDR compliance, disable tracing globally or per-run.</p>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="python"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Option B: Disable per-run using RunConfig</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> agents </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Runner, RunConfig</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Create a config with tracing disabled</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">zdr_config </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> RunConfig(</span><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">tracing_disabled</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">True</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Run without tracing</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">result </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Runner.run(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    pe_concierge,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    "What's our MOIC on the TechCorp investment?"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    run_config</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">zdr_config</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">f</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"Response: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">{</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">result.final_output[:</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">200</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">]</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">}</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">..."</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">✓ No trace data sent to OpenAI for this run."</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span></code></pre>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="text"><code><span class="line"><span>Response: I can calculate it, but I need to pull the latest TechCorp valuation and our invested capital from the portfolio metrics.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>To make sure I’m looking at the right record, which “TechCorp” do you mean (e...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>✓ No trace data sent to OpenAI for this run.</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="option-2-custom-trace-processors-internal-observability" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Option 2: Custom Trace Processors (Internal
