<ul>
<li><strong>Promptfoo</strong>: Free, open source (<a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo">MIT license</a>)</li>
<li><strong>Email verification</strong>: One-time free email check on first run (spam prevention, not a subscription)</li>
<li><strong>LLM cost</strong>: Your standard OpenAI API usage for attack generation + grading. With <code>numTests: 10</code> across ~9 plugins, expect ~100-200 API calls (a few dollars)</li>
<li><strong>No subscription required</strong> — your existing <code>OPENAI_API_KEY</code> is all you need</li>
</ul>

19.7071C1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 12.8926 4.29289 10.2929L5.29289 9.29289C5.68341 8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 6.7071 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>Promptfoo needs a way to talk to your governed agent. The file <code>promptfoo/promptfoo_target.py</code> bridges Promptfoo to your <code>GuardrailAgent</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Receives each adversarial prompt from Promptfoo</li>
<li>Runs it through <code>Runner.run(pe_concierge_governed, prompt)</code> - the full agent with handoffs, tools, and centralized guardrails</li>
<li>Returns the response, or <code>[BLOCKED]</code> if any guardrail fires</li>
</ul>
<p>The script recreates the same agent stack from the notebook: specialist agents, tools, custom <code>pe_guardrail</code>, <code>PE_FIRM_POLICY</code>, and the <code>GuardrailAgent</code> triage agent.</p>

<p>The file <code>promptfoo/promptfooconfig.yaml</code> defines what to attack and how:</p>
<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="yaml"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">targets</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> - </span><span style="color:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">id</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"python:promptfoo/promptfoo_target.py"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">    label</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"pe-concierge-governed"</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">purpose</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">></span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  # Application context improves attack quality</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">  A Private Equity firm front-desk AI assistant that handles deal screening,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">  portfolio management, and investor relations...</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">redteam</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">  numTests</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">10</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  # Adversarial inputs per plugin</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">  plugins</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:                     </span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Generate adversarial inputs</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">hijacking</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">                # Off-topic hijacking</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">pii:direct</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">               # PII extraction attempts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">prompt-extraction</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">        # System prompt extraction</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">system-prompt-override</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">   # Override system instructions</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">off-topic</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">                # Off-topic manipulation</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">policy</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">                   # Custom policy violations</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">  strategies</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:                  </span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Wrap inputs in evasion techniques</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">jailbreak</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">                # Jailbreak wrapper patterns</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">prompt-injection</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">         # Injection wrapper patterns</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">base64</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">                   # Base64 encoding evasion</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">leetspeak</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">                # l33tspeak encoding</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">rot13</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">                    # ROT13 encoding evasion</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   - </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">crescendo</span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">                # Gradually escalating attacks</span></span></code></pre>
<p><strong>Plugins</strong> generate adversarial inputs targeting specific vulnerabilities. <strong>Strategies</strong> wrap those inputs in evasion techniques (jailbreak patterns, encoding, translation) to test whether guardrails can be bypassed beyond simple text matching. See the <a href="https://www.promptfoo.dev/docs/red-team/plugins/">full plugin list</a> for 131 available plugins.</p>

<pre class="astro-code astro-code-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8; overflow-x: auto;" tabindex="0" data-language="bash"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Navigate to the promptfoo directory</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">cd</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> promptfoo</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Generate adversarial inputs and run them against your agent</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">promptfoo</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> redteam</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> run</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># View the interactive report</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">promptfoo</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> redteam</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> report</span></span></code></pre>
<p>The report shows:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Pass/fail rate</strong> per vulnerability category</li>
<li><strong>Severity levels</strong> for each finding</li>
<li><strong>Concrete examples</strong> of inputs that bypassed guardrails</li>
<li><strong>Suggested mitigations</strong> for each vulnerability</li>
</ul>

<p>This demo used 5 plugins with <code>numTests: 3</code> for a quick 33-probe scan. For production-grade assessments, increase the depth to 50+ probes per plugin and enable preset collections like <code>owasp:llm</code> (OWASP LLM Top 10), <code>nist:ai:measure</code> (NIST AI RMF), or <code>mitre:atlas</code> — Promptfoo supports 131 plugins across security, compliance, trust &#x26; safety, and brand categories.</p>

Governance enables adoption</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info focus-visible:opacity-100 group-focus-within:opacity-100 focus-visible:outline focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-gray-300 group-hover:opacity-100 dark:focus-visible:outline-gray-600 motion-reduce:transition-none relative -top-0.5" data-anchor-id="1-governance-enables-adoption" aria-label="Copy link to 1. <p>By establishing clear guardrails upfront, you remove the fear and uncertainty that slows AI adoption. Teams can build confidently knowing policies are enforced automatically. Governance becomes an execution system that keeps adoption moving securely and at scale.</p>
<h3 id="2-use-handoffs-for-specialization" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">2. <p>Avoid one massive agent. Create specialists and let them collaborate. The <code>handoff_description</code> is key to good routing.</p>

<ul>
<li><strong>OpenAI Guardrails</strong> (client-level): Universal policies for all calls</li>
<li><strong>Agents SDK guardrails</strong> (agent-level): Domain-specific validation</li>
</ul>

<p>The policy-as-a-package pattern lets you:</p>
<ul>

fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>When moving from prototype to production, consider how different user groups will interact with AI:</p>

























<table><thead><tr><th>Role</th><th>What They Build</th><th>Governance Approach</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><strong>Developers</strong></td><td>Custom agents, MCP connectors, integrations</td><td>Safe defaults, reusable templates, evaluation pipelines</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Power Users</strong></td><td>Configured assistants, automated workflows</td><td>Pre-approved patterns, governed portals</td></tr><tr><td><strong>End Users</strong></td><td>Content generation, data analysis</td><td>Curated tools with embedded guardrails</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>This approach ensures everyone, from engineers to analysts, can leverage AI safely within appropriate boundaries.</p>
<h3 id="enabling-citizen-developers" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Enabling Citizen Developers</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 <p>Empower non-technical teams to build safely:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Provide templates</strong> for prompt packs, tool configurations, and evaluation checks</li>
<li><strong>Create review lanes</strong> and publishing workflows that make it easy to build and deploy</li>
<li><strong>Offer guardrailed sandboxes</strong> for experimentation without risking sensitive data</li>
<li><strong>Establish clear promotion paths</strong> from prototype to production with governance checkpoints</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="registries-for-visibility" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Registries for Visibility</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info focus-visible:opacity-100 <p>Treat AI assets as first-class governed resources by maintaining registries:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Agent Registry</strong>: Register all agents with owner, purpose, risk tier, and evaluation status</li>
<li><strong>Tool Registry</strong>: Document MCP tools with authentication scopes, data access, and approval authority</li>
<li><strong>Prompt Registry</strong>: Version and govern prompts like code, with lineage, rollback policies, and change controls</li>
</ul>
<p>Registry metadata enables discoverability, auditing, and lifecycle management across your AI ecosystem.</p>
<h3 id="risk-proportionate-controls" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Risk-Proportionate Controls</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info focus-visible:opacity-100 Controls"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" aria-hidden="true" class="h-3.5 w-3.5"><path d="M18.2929 5.7071C16.4743 3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 <p>Not all AI use cases carry the same risk. Differentiate your controls:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Low-risk</strong> (internal productivity, non-sensitive data): Fast-track approval, minimal logging</li>
<li><strong>Moderate-risk</strong> (customer-facing, operational data): Standard guardrails, audit trails</li>
<li><strong>High-risk</strong> (PII, financial, regulated): Enhanced logging, human-in-the-loop, isolated environments</li>
</ul>
<p>Apply proportionate controls, approvals, review, and detailed logging, only where necessary, keeping lightweight adoption fast and frictionless.</p>
<h3 id="preventing-shadow-ai" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Preventing Shadow AI</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-0.5 opacity-0 transition-colors transition-opacity duration-200 ease-out text-info hover:text-info focus-visible:opacity-100 <p>Centralized governance helps prevent unauthorized AI tools from proliferating:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Make governed options easier</strong> than ungoverned alternatives</li>
<li><strong>Provide clear adoption paths</strong> for different skill levels and use cases</li>
<li><strong>Incorporate discovery mechanisms</strong> to detect and catalog unsanctioned AI activity</li>
<li><strong>Offer support and training</strong> so teams don’t go around the system</li>
</ul>
<p>Early visibility allows governance teams to close gaps before they become systemic risks.</p>
<h3 id="standards-alignment" class="group flex items-center gap-1 mt-7 mb-2 scroll-mt-[110px]"><span class="min-w-0">Standards Alignment</span><button type="button" class="shrink-0 self-center <p>Align your governance practices with recognized frameworks:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>NIST AI RMF</strong> - Risk management framework for AI systems</li>
<li><strong>ISO/IEC 42001</strong> - AI management system standard</li>
<li><strong>Industry-specific requirements</strong> (HIPAA, SOX, GDPR, etc.)</li>
</ul>
<p>Building on established standards creates external credibility alongside internal control.</p>
<hr>

    const copyHeadingLink = async (slug) => {
      const url = `${location.origin}${location.pathname}#${slug}`;
      if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText) {
        try {
          await navigator.clipboard.writeText(url);
          return;
        } catch (error) {
          console.warn("Copy to clipboard failed", error);
        }
      }

      window.prompt("Copy link", url);
    };

    document.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      const target = event.target;
      if (!(target instanceof Element)) return;

      const button = target.closest("[data-anchor-id]");
      if (!button) return;

      const slug = button.getAttribute("data-anchor-id");
      if (!slug) return;

      event.preventDefault();
      copyHeadingLink(slug);
      const heading = document.getElementById(slug);
      if (heading) {
        heading.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "start" });
      }
      history.replaceState(null, "", `#${slug}`);
